***стыть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стыть.html>стыть</a> (14116)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стыть.html>стыть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stytʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остыть.html>осты́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to be getting cool / cold; to be cooling down</li>
<li>to freeze, to be frozen, to be cold
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:кровь.html>кровь</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:стыть.html>сты́нет</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жила.html>жи́лах</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">krovʹ <b>stýnet</b> v žílax</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one's blood freezes, one's blood runs cold, it makes one's blood curdle</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">сты́нуть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stýnutʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">to cool down</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:остывать.html>остыва́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">ostyvátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стычка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стычка.html>сты́чка</a> (12286)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Per Dal, from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стыка́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stykátʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to connect, to join</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; presumably the sense development was "joining" → "meeting" → "skirmishing".
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стычка.html>сты́чка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stýčka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стычка.html>сты́чки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стычка.html>сты́чки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стычка.html>сты́чек</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>skirmish (brief battle between small groups)</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стюард.html>стюард</a> (31326)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">steward</i>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***стяг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стяг.html>стяг</a> (27332)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">стѧгъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stęgŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which is most probably from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old Norse</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">stǫng</i> (whence <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">stang</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">stang</i>). Compare <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:штанга.html>шта́нга</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">štánga</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Stange</i>. Alternative reconstructions point towards <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*stěgъ</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">сцяг</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">scjah</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk"><a href = vnd.unilang:стяг.html>стяг</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stjah</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стяг.html>стяг</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stjag</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стяг.html>стя́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стяг.html>стя́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стяг.html>стя́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic<span class="ib-comma">,</span> literary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> banner, flag</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***стягивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стягивать.html>стя́гивать</a> (11577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">стяг-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">stjag-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ивать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ivatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стягивать.html>стя́гивать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stjágivatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стянуть.html>стяну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten, to tie up, to strap down/up</li>
<li>to gather, to draw up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стягивать.html>стя́гивать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stjágivatʹ</b> síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw up forces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pull off/away</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стягиваться.html>стя́гиваться</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stjágivatʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стяну́ться</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stjanútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">стягива́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">stjagivánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***стянуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:стянуть.html>стяну́ть</a> (6399)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">с-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">s-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:тянуть.html>тяну́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">tjanútʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стянуть.html>стяну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">stjanútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:стягивать.html>стя́гивать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to tighten, to tie up, to strap down/up</li>
<li>to gather, to draw up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:стянуть.html>стяну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сила.html>си́лы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>stjanútʹ</b> síly</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to draw up forces</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to pull off/away</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to filch, to swipe, to pinch</li></ol>

***суббота.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́та</a> (3020)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">субота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">subota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Greek">Byzantine Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">*σάμβατον</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*sámbaton</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σάββατα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sábbata</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aramaic" class="extiw" title="w:Aramaic">Aramaic</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="arc">שַׁבְּתָא</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="arc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šabbǝtā</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Hebrew_language" class="extiw" title="w:Hebrew language">Hebrew</a></span> <i class="Hebr mention" lang="he">שַׁבָּת</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="he-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">šabbāt</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The <b>-бб-</b> arose from the influence of <b>-bb-</b> in the Western languages.
</p><p>Near cognates: <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">субо́та</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">subóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Belarusian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Belarusian language">Belarusian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="be">субо́та</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="be-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">subóta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Church_Slavonic" class="extiw" title="w:Old Church Slavonic">Old Church Slavonic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">сѫбота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sǫbota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bulgarian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Bulgarian language">Bulgarian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="bg">съ́бота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="bg-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sǎ́bota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Serbo-Croatian" class="extiw" title="w:Serbo-Croatian">Serbo-Croatian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="sh">су́бота</i>.
</p><p>But also there is Old Church Slavonic <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="cu">собота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="cu-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sobota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (Czech, Slovak, Polish, Polabian, Lower Sorbian <i class="Latn mention" lang="dsb">sobota</i>) that is from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sabbatum</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">σάββατα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sábbata</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́та</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">subbóta</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ты</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́т</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Saturday
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ту</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>subbótu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Saturday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́там</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">po <b>subbótam</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">on Saturdays</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:к.html>к</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́те</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">k <b>subbóte</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">by Saturday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ты</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s <b>subbóty</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from Saturday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:пятница.html>пя́тницы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ты</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">s pjátnicy do <b>subbóty</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">from Friday to Saturday</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:следующий.html>сле́дующую</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́ту</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v slédujuščuju <b>subbótu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">next Saturday</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***субботник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:субботник.html>суббо́тник</a> (20225)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суббота.html>суббо́та</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">subbóta</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">Saturday</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, since 1919 when the first subbotnik was held.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:субботник.html>суббо́тник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">subbótnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:субботник.html>суббо́тника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:субботник.html>суббо́тники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:субботник.html>суббо́тников</a></b>)
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суд</a> (798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сꙋдъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sudŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sǫdъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суд</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sud</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суда́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суды́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>судо́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> court</li>

<li>tribunal</li>

***сударыня.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рыня</a> (15012)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Feminine form of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́дарь</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">súdarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Also, contracted form of <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государыня.html>госуда́рыня</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">gosudárynja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рыня</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sudárynja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рыни</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рыни</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рынь</a></b>, <i>masculine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́дарь</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>madam, milady</li></ol>

***сударь.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́дарь</a> (7198)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Contracted form of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:государь.html>госуда́рь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">gosudárʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sire</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Rather archaic.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́дарь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">súdarʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́даря</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́дари</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударь.html>су́дарей</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сударыня.html>суда́рыня</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>sir</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not in common use since 1917. Despite some attempts, the political reforms in Russia and other Ex-USSR states have not revived the word. Still found in older fiction and is used by some speakers.</li></ul>

***судебный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:судебный.html>суде́бный</a> (4427)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">судьбьныи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sudĭbĭnyi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, synchronically analysable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́бный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ébnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судебный.html>суде́бный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sudébnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>judicial, judiciary <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to a court of law</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:судебный.html>суде́бный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:надзор.html>надзо́р</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sudébnyj</b> nadzór</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>judicial</b> review</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>forensic
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:судебный.html>суде́бная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:медицина.html>медици́на</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sudébnaja</b> medicína</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>forensic</b> medicine</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***судить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>суди́ть</a> (977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">судити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">suditi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sǭdìti</i>. See also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:суд.html>суд</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sud</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>суди́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sudítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to judge, to try, to adjudicate
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1958</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mikhail_Aleksandrovich_Sholokhov" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mikhail Aleksandrovich Sholokhov">Mikhail Aleksandrovich Sholokhov</a>,  <cite><a href = vnd.unilang:поднятый.html>по́днятая</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:целина.html>целина́</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>его́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:исключить.html>исключи́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:комсомол.html>комсомо́ла</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>суди́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хулиганство.html>хулига́нство</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:за.html>за</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:поджог.html>поджо́г</a>.</span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jevó isključíli iz komsomóla, <b>sudíli</b> za xuligánstvo i za podžóg.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">He was expelled from the Komsomol, was <b>tried</b> for disorderly conduct (hooliganism) and for arson.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li>to judge <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">to form an opinion on</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:стараться.html>стара́юсь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:беспристрастный.html>беспристра́стно</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>суди́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:о.html>о</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:человек.html>лю́дях</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja starájusʹ bespristrástno <b>sudítʹ</b> o ljúdjax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm trying to <b>judge</b> people impartially.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:судить.html>су́дя</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>всему́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>súdja</b> po vsemú</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to all appearances</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">poetic or dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to destine, to predetermine</li></ol>
